. *para sacar LMR 
.         *https://www.statalist.org/forums/forum/general-stata-discussion/general/1412686-calculating-entropy-for-lca-
> latent-class-analysis-in-stata-15/page3
. program lmrtest, rclass
  1.         version 15.0
  2.         args estimates_null estimates_alternative
  3.         tempname n ll_null ll_alt parms_null parms_alt a classes_null classes_alt lr_test_stat modlr_test_stat p q
  4.         quietly {
  5.         estimates restore `1'
  6.         scalar `n' = e(N)
  7.         scalar `ll_null' = e(ll)
  8.         scalar `parms_null' = e(K)
  9.         matrix `a' = e(lclass_k_levels)
 10.         scalar `classes_null' = `a'[1,1]
 11.         estimates restore `2'
 12.         scalar `ll_alt' = e(ll)
 13.         scalar `parms_alt' = e(K)
 14.         matrix `a' = e(lclass_k_levels)
 15.         scalar `classes_alt' = `a'[1,1]
 16.         scalar `p' = (3 * `classes_alt' - 1)
 17.         scalar `q' = (3 * `classes_null' - 1)
 18.         scalar `lr_test_stat' = -2 * (`ll_null' - `ll_alt')
 19.         scalar `modlr_test_stat' = `lr_test_stat' / (1 + ((`p' - `q') * ln(`n')) ^ -1)
 20.         }
 21.         return scalar lmrt_p = chi2tail(`parms_alt' - `parms_null',`modlr_test_stat')
 22.         end
